{"answers": ["An elevator with a counterbalance"], "model_answer": "A real-world application of an Atwood machine is an elevator with a counterbalance. An elevator with a counterbalance approximates an ideal Atwood machine and thereby relieves the driving motor from the load of holding the elevator cab - it has to overcome only the weight difference and inertia of the two masses. This principle is also used for funicular railways with two connected railway cars on inclined tracks, and for the elevators on the Eiffel Tower which counterbalance each other."}
